	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: 3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf');
	$tmp = pathinfo('3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}

	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): 3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf');
} else if (sha1_file('3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf') != '95b72a2b9ce760ffd24dccd2103e69832ddf3a82') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): 3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of 3p/vts_fileformats/filetypes.conf');
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '896d719e8125fcf24d30f07ad2a64f99379042cf') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '896d719e8125fcf24d30f07ad2a64f99379042cf') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '24c6f42b6b6e64806904b66e6342e8c4de228696') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '896d719e8125fcf24d30f07ad2a64f99379042cf') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') != 'd36c3f45166c2f17db67f958a5286725120de40e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/oidplus.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') !== 'd36c3f45166c2f17db67f958a5286725120de40e') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') !== 'a2f0f14e14f2008f352f6504aecb5d97eef73553') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/oidplus.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/oidplus.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/oidplus.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/oidplus.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') !== 'd36c3f45166c2f17db67f958a5286725120de40e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('update/index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: update/index.php');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('update/index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): update/index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('update/index.php') != 'c54e5cea8e7d1ba63d83c3c67abe49a3a1efeb62') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): update/index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('update/index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of update/index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== 'c54e5cea8e7d1ba63d83c3c67abe49a3a1efeb62') {
		if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== 'a7b8467fd94b19e6ed34fc9cade39dac40aab632') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: update/index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('update/index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('update/index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('update/index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== 'c54e5cea8e7d1ba63d83c3c67abe49a3a1efeb62') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): update/index.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 488\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 488') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');
